<script>
	$j("#login-registrazione").click(function(){
		//alert("asdasd");
		gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({
			screenSet:'LSMainPanels-RegistrationLogin', 
			onError: 'errorHandler',
			mobileScreenSet:''
		});
	});
	
	$j(".utente-profilo").click(function(){
		$j(".utente-menu").addClass("hidden");
		
		gigya.accounts.showScreenSet({
			screenSet:'LSMainPanels-ProfileUpdate', 
			onError: 'errorHandler',
			mobileScreenSet:''
		});
	});
	
	function errorHandler(eventObj) {
	    alert("failed with error" + eventObj.eventName);
	    //Some error handling
	}
</script>

<script>
	var obj = "";

    function onLoad() {
        // register for login event
        gigya.accounts.addEventHandlers({
                onLogin: onLoginHandler, 
                onLogout: onLogoutHandler
        });
        
        userInfo(userCheck);
    }
    //onLogin Event handler
    function onLoginHandler(eventObj) {
    	console.log(eventObj)
    	$j.ajax({
		  	method: "GET",

		  	url: "/modulo/gigya/jsp/check-abbonato-edizioni-cookie.jsp",

		  	data: { uguid: eventObj.UID },
		  	cache: false
		}).done(function( msg ) {		    
//		    var esito = $j.parseJSON(msg);
//		    if(esito.ReturnCode == 200){
		    	gigya.setSSOToken({redirectURL: window.location.href});
//		    }
		});
    }
    
    function onLogoutHandler(eventObj) {
        window.location.reload();
    }
    
    $j(".utente-logout").click(function(){
    	logoutFromGS();
    });
    
    // Logout from Gigya platform. This method is activated when "Logout" button is clicked
    function logoutFromGS() {
    	
    	setCookie("LStp_mcp_UTP", "false", -1);
    	setCookie("_aToken", "false", -1);
    	setCookie("_gToken", "false", -1);
    	
    	$j.ajax({
		  	method: "GET",
		  	url: "/modulo/gigya/jsp/logout-session.jsp",
		  	cache: false
		}).done(function( msg ) {
		    gigya.accounts.logout(); // logout from Gigya platform
		});
    	
        
    }

    var userInfo = function (callbackP) {
		gigya.socialize.getUserInfo({callback: callbackP, extraFields: 'languages, address, phones, education, honors, publications, patents, cert qifications, professionalHeadline, bio, industry, specialties, work, skills, religion, politicalView, interestedIn, relationshipStatus, hometown, favorites, likes, username, locale, verified, irank, timezone'});
	}
	
	var userCheck = function (response) {

		var user = response ? response['user'] : undefined;

		if (user !== undefined) {  
			if (user['UID'].length > 0 ) {
				
				checkCookies(user);
				renderUI(user);
				return;
				
			} else {
				//console.log("Error: " + response.errorMessage);
			}
			
		}else{
			//console.log("no user");
		}
	}
	
	var renderUI = function(obj){

		if(obj){
			if(obj.thumbnailURL != ""){
				$j(".foto-utente img").attr("src", obj.thumbnailURL);
			}else{
				$j(".foto-utente img").attr("src", "/modulo/gigya/img/profile_default_pic_small.png");
			}
			
	        $j(".nome-utente").html(obj.firstName);
	        
	        $j(".contenitore-utente").removeClass("hidden");
	        $j("#login-registrazione").addClass("hidden");
		}else{
			$j(".contenitore-utente").addClass("hidden");
			$j("#login-registrazione").removeClass("hidden");
		}
		
		
	}
	
	var checkCookies = function(user){

		if (user['UID'].length > 0 && getCookie("_aToken").length == 0 && getCookie("_gToken").length == 0) {
			$j.ajax({
			  	method: "GET",
	
			  	url: "/modulo/gigya/jsp/check-abbonato-edizioni-cookie.jsp",
	
			  	data: { uguid: user['UID'] },
			  	cache: false
			}).done(function( msg ) {
			    gigya.setSSOToken({redirectURL: window.location.href});
			});
		}else{
			//logoutFromGS();
		}
	}
	
	onLoad();
	
	$j(".utente-menu-trigger").on("click", function(){
		if($j(".utente-menu").hasClass("hidden")){
			$j(".utente-menu").removeClass("hidden");
		}else{
			$j(".utente-menu").addClass("hidden");
		}
	});	
</script>

			$j("#facebook_placeholder, #google_placeholder, #twitter_placeholder").unbind();
		
			$j("#facebook_placeholder").click(function(e){
				
				e.preventDefault();

				if($j(this).hasClass("clicked")){
					closeSocialItem(this);
				}else{
					closeSocialItem($j("#twitter_placeholder"));
					closeSocialItem($j("#google_placeholder"));
					openSocialItem(this);
				}
			});
			
			$j("#google_placeholder").click(function(e){
				
				e.preventDefault();

				if($j(this).hasClass("clicked")){
					closeSocialItem(this);
				}else{
					closeSocialItem($j("#twitter_placeholder"));
					closeSocialItem($j("#facebook_placeholder"));
					openSocialItem(this);
				}
			});
			
			$j("#twitter_placeholder").click(function(e){
				
				e.preventDefault();

				if($j(this).hasClass("clicked")){
					closeSocialItem(this);
				}else{
					closeSocialItem($j("#google_placeholder"));
					closeSocialItem($j("#facebook_placeholder"));
					openSocialItem(this);
				}
			});
			
			function openSocialItem(item){

				if(!$j(item).hasClass("clicked")){
					var imgWidth = 25;
					var share_container_width = $j(item).find(".share_container").width();
					
					$j(item).addClass("clicked");
						
					$j(item).animate({
						width: imgWidth + share_container_width + 15
					}, 300);
				}
			}
			
			function closeSocialItem(item){

				if($j(item).hasClass("clicked")){
					var imgWidth = 25;
					var share_container_width = $j(item).find(".share_container").width();
					
					$j(item).removeClass("clicked");
						
					$j(item).animate({
						width: imgWidth
					}, 200);
				}
			}
			
			//.ls-topBannerSearch
			
			$j(document).ready(function(){
				//$j(".ls-topBannerSearch").after($j("#top_share_link"));
				//$j("#top_share_link").fadeIn(200);
			});
			
			
		</script>

<script>
$j("#ilsecolo-edizioni span:eq(0)").bind(
	"click",
	function () {
		var w = 360;
		if ($j("#ilsecolo-edizioni").width() < 200) {
			$j("#menuVCO").html("VCO");			
		}
		else {
			w = 159;
		}
		$j("#ilsecolo-edizioni").animate (
			{width:w+"px"},
			1000, function() {
				if ($j("#ilsecolo-edizioni").width() < 200) {
					$j("#menuVCO").html("VERBANO CUSIO OSSOLA");
					$j("#ilsecolo-edizioni span b").html("&lt;")
				}
				else {
					$j("#ilsecolo-edizioni span b").html("&gt;")
				}
			}
		)
	}
)

</script>

<article data-uuid="7357b334-73ee-11e9-9d09-515a81661719" class="flex-boxitem-story" is="ls-article-story">
	<header>

	$j( document ).ready(function() {
		var strAltezze = "|";
		
		if(!device.mobile()){
			$j("ls-flexbox").each(function( index ) {
				if($j(this).attr("data-cols")>1 && typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") == "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
					});
		
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").height(arrAltezze[0]);
				}else if(typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") !== "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
						}
					});
					
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							$j(this).height(arrAltezze[0]);
						}
					});
				}
			});
		}
	});

<script>
	$j( document ).ready(function() {
		var strAltezze = "|";
		
		if(!device.mobile()){
			$j("ls-flexbox").each(function( index ) {
				if($j(this).attr("data-cols")>1 && typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") == "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
					});
		
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").height(arrAltezze[0]);
				}else if(typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") !== "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
						}
					});
					
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							$j(this).height(arrAltezze[0]);
						}
					});
				}
			});
		}
	}); 
</script></div>

<script>
	function abbonamento(link){
		location.href=link;
	};
	
	function selTab(quale) {
		var insertRotatorLOW = $j("#insertRotatorLOW");
		$j(".label", insertRotatorLOW).removeClass("sel");
		$j(".rotatorItem", insertRotatorLOW).removeClass("sel");

		$j("#label-" + quale, insertRotatorLOW).addClass("sel");
		$j("#rotator-" + quale, insertRotatorLOW).addClass("sel");
		
		$j("#rotator-" + quale + " .ls-box-image img", insertRotatorLOW).unveil();
	}
	$j(function() {
		var insertRotatorLOW = $j("#insertRotatorLOW").detach();
		insertRotatorLOW.insertBefore($j(".ls-colonna1A .ls-box-object:last"));
		insertRotatorLOW.show();
		$j(".rotatorItem", insertRotatorLOW).each(
			function() {
				var abbX = $j(".abbX", this).detach();
				$j(".ls-box-text", this).append(abbX);
				$j(".ls-box-sommario", this).remove();
			}
		);
		$j(".ls-box-image img", insertRotatorLOW).unveil();
	});
</script>

<script>
	$j( document ).ready(function() {
		var strAltezze = "|";
		
		if(!device.mobile()){
			$j("ls-flexbox").each(function( index ) {
				if($j(this).attr("data-cols")>1 && typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") == "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
					});
		
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").height(arrAltezze[0]);
				}else if(typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") !== "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
						}
					});
					
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							$j(this).height(arrAltezze[0]);
						}
					});
				}
			});
		}
	}); 
</script></div>
<script>
(function ( $ ) {
	$.fn.col1BHP = function() {
	   	this[0].orientationChanged = function() {
     		this.render();
     	}

		this[0].render = function () {
			var Col1B = $j(".ls-colonna1B").detach();
			if (device.landscape()) {
				Col1B.css("margin-top", "0rem");
				Col1B.insertBefore($j(".ls-colonna1A"));
			}
			else {
				Col1B.css("margin-top", "1rem");
				Col1B.insertBefore($j(".ls-colonna1A .ls-box-object:eq(4)"));
			}
		}
		
		registerOCL(this[0]);
	}
	if (device.mobile() && device.portrait()) {
		var Col1B = $j(".ls-colonna1B");
		Col1B.col1BHP();
		Col1B[0].orientationChanged();
	}
}( jQuery ));

<script>
	$j( document ).ready(function() {
		var strAltezze = "|";
		
		if(!device.mobile()){
			$j("ls-flexbox").each(function( index ) {
				if($j(this).attr("data-cols")>1 && typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") == "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
					});
		
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").height(arrAltezze[0]);
				}else if(typeof $j(this).attr("data-layout-map") !== "undefined"){
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							strAltezze =  strAltezze + "," + $j(this).height()
						}
					});
					
					var arrAltezze = strAltezze.replace("|,", "").split(",");
					arrAltezze.sort(function(a, b){return b-a});
					
					//console.log("arrAltezze => " + arrAltezze[0]);
					//console.log("uuid ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("id"));
					//console.log("layout ls-flexbox => " + $j(this).attr("data-layout-map"));
					
					$j(this).find("article").each(function( index ) {
						if(index > 0){
							$j(this).height(arrAltezze[0]);
						}
					});
				}
			});
		}
	});

<script>
if (device.mobile()) {
	$j(function() {
		var BoxMMulti = $j("#UUID-31dfd942-d04f-11e8-b9e6-f22ce9c0fd9f").detach();
		var posizione = "insertBefore|.ls-colonna1A .ls-box-object:eq(0)";
		var meth = "";
		if (posizione.length == 0) {
			posizione = ".ls-colonna1A .ls-box-object:eq(3)";
		}
		else {
			var toks = posizione.split("|");
			if (toks.length == 2) {
				meth = toks[0];
				posizione = toks[1];
			}
		}
		if (meth == "insertBefore") {
			BoxMMulti.insertBefore(posizione);
		}
		else {
			BoxMMulti.insertAfter(posizione);			
		}
		$j("#theWallX img", BoxMMulti).unveil();
	});
}

<script>
	var layer = getCookie("layer");
	var layerls = getCookie("layer").length;
	
	function getCookie(cname) {
		var name = cname + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		for(var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
			if (c.indexOf(name) != -1) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
		}
		return "";
	} 
</script>

	var larghezzaImgTTX = $j(".imgTTX").width();
	var altezzaImgTTX = (larghezzaImgTTX * 9)/16;
	$j(".imgTTX").height(altezzaImgTTX);
	$j(".tsaImgColorata").height(altezzaImgTTX);
	$j(".tsaImgColorata").width(larghezzaImgTTX);
	$j(".tguImgColorata").height(altezzaImgTTX);

	var larghezzaEspandi = $j(".espandiTTX .piuTTX").width() + $j(".espandiTTX .labelTTX").width(); 
	var centraturaEspandi = (larghezzaBody - larghezzaEspandi)/2;
	$j(".espandiTTX").attr("style", "padding-left:"+centraturaEspandi+"px"); 
	$j(".riduciTTX").attr("style", "padding-left:"+centraturaEspandi+"px"); 

	
	$j(".espandiTTX").click(function(){
		$j(".tuttiXmobile").hide();
		$j(".tuttiXdesktop").show();
		$j(".riduciTTX").show();
		$j(".tuttiXdesktop .ls-box-object img").unveil(true);
		$j("html").attr("style", "overflow:hidden;");
		$j("body").attr("style", "overflow:hidden;position:fixed;");
	});
	
	$j(".riduciTTX").click(function(){
		$j(".tuttiXmobile").show();
		$j(".tuttiXdesktop").hide();
		$j(".riduciTTX").hide();
		$j("html").removeAttr("style");
		$j("body").removeAttr("style");
		             
		document.getElementById('tuttiXmobile').scrollIntoView();            
	});

<script type="text/javascript">
	var edicola_sezione=$j("#edicola_sezione");	
	
	function ricerca_notizie(sez_edicola){
		$j.ajax({
		  type: "get",
		  url: "/modulo/edicola/ajax/titoli-giornale.jpt",
		  dataType: 'json',
		  data: {
		  	'section': sez_edicola
		  	},
		  cache: false,
		  complete: function(xhr){
		  	document.getElementById('articoli_edicola').innerHTML = xhr.responseText;
		  }
		});
	}
	
	
	edicola_sezione.change(function(){
		ricerca_notizie(edicola_sezione.val());
	});
</script><script>

	function loadChartbeat() {
		window._sf_endpt=(new Date()).getTime();
		var e = document.createElement('script');
		e.setAttribute('language', 'javascript');
		e.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
		if (media_type == "video") {
			e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat_video.js');
//			e.setAttribute('src', 'http://pages.chartbeat.com/video/video_debug.js');
		}
		else {
			e.setAttribute('src', '//static.chartbeat.com/js/chartbeat.js');
		}
		document.body.appendChild(e);
	}
	var oldonload = window.onload;
	window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function') ?
		loadChartbeat : function() { oldonload(); loadChartbeat(); };
})();
